if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') != '340da6d572b2074900607b5336e40593dcc05d18') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') !== '340da6d572b2074900607b5336e40593dcc05d18') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') !== 'c62e27cf1d43ccebbbcc8c5de16669e9f1462d86') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php') !== '340da6d572b2074900607b5336e40593dcc05d18') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusConfig.class.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') != 'c085740caef3366dac228bb83edd61cb1bd09f16') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'c085740caef3366dac228bb83edd61cb1bd09f16') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '4c3bdd536ac8f3eb4a0cc954f9bf562e9e1ab80a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== 'c085740caef3366dac228bb83edd61cb1bd09f16') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}
